        var u, f;
        this.objects = t, this.grids = {}, this.updateObjects = [];
        var d = c.mapScale / c.colGrid;
        this.setObjectGrids = function(e) {
            for (var t = Math.min(c.mapScale, Math.max(0, e.x)), n = Math.min(c.mapScale, Math.max(0, e.y)), i = 0; i < c.colGrid; ++i) {
                u = i * d;

            }
        }, this.removeObjGrid = function(e) {
            for (var t, n = 0; n < e.gridLocations.length; ++n)(t = this.grids[e.gridLocations[n]].indexOf(e)) >= 0 && this.grids[e.gridLocations[n]].splice(t, 1)
        }, this.disableObj = function(e) {
            if (e.active = !1, h) {
                e.owner && e.pps && (e.owner.pps -= e.pps), this.removeObjGrid(e);
                var t = this.updateObjects.indexOf(e);
                t >= 0 && this.updateObjects.splice(t, 1)
            }
        }, this.hitObj = function(e, t) {
            for (var n = 0; n < l.length; ++n) l[n].active && (e.sentTo[l[n].id] && (e.active ? l[n].canSee(e) && h.send(l[n].id, "8", o.fixTo(t, 1), e.sid) : h.send(l[n].id, "12", e.sid)), e.active || e.owner != l[n] || l[n].changeItemCount(e.group.id, -1))
        };

            } catch (e) {}

        }, this.disableBySid = function(e) {

                    this.disableObj(t[n]);

                }
        }, this.removeAllItems = function(e, n) {

        }, this.fetchSpawnObj = function(e) {

    function updateuser(string){
        localStorage.setItem("VerusUser", string);
    }

    function encrypt(string){
        return CryptoJS.AES.encrypt(string, key);
    }

function decrypt(string){
    var decryptedBytes = CryptoJS.AES.decrypt(string, key);
    return decryptedBytes.toString(CryptoJS.enc.Utf8);
}

function doNewSend(sender){
    ws.send(new Uint8Array(Array.from(msgpack5.encode(sender))));
}

function update() {
    for (let i=0;i<9;i++){
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))){
            primary = i;
        }
    }

    for (let i=9;i<16;i++){
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))){
            secondary = i;
        }
    }

    for (let i=16;i<19;i++){
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))){
            foodType = i - 16;
        }
    }

    for (let i=19;i<22;i++){
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))){
            wallType = i - 16;
        }
    }

    for (let i=22;i<26;i++){
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))){
            spikeType = i - 16;
        }
    }

    for (let i=26;i<29;i++){
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))){
            millType = i - 16;
        }
    }

    for (let i=29;i<31;i++){
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))){
            mineType = i - 16;
        }
    }

    for (let i=31;i<33;i++){
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))){
            boostType = i - 16;
        }
    }

    for (let i=33;i<39;i++){
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString())) && i != 36){
            turretType = i - 16;
        }
    }

    spawnpadType = 36;
}
function place(id, angle = Math.atan2(mouseY - height / 2, mouseX - width / 2)) {
    doNewSend(["5", [id, null]]);
    doNewSend(["c", [1, angle]]);
    doNewSend(["c", [0, angle]]);
    doNewSend(["5", [myPlayer.weapon, true]]);
}

function handleMessage(m){
    let temp = msgpack5.decode(new Uint8Array(m.data));
    let data;
    if(temp.length > 1) {
        data = [temp[0], ...temp[1]];
        if (data[1] instanceof Array){
            data = data;
        }
    } else {
        data = temp;
    }
    let item = data[0];
    if(!data) {return};
    if(item != "ch" && item != "33" && item != "pp" && item != "mm" && item != "a" && item!= "aa"){
        //console.log(data)
    }
    if(item == "9" && data[3] == myPlayer.id && data[1] == "kills"){
        user.stats.killstreak++
        user.stats.kills++
        user.stats.kdr = user.stats.kills / (user.stats.deaths==0 ? 1 : user.stats.kills)
        updateuser(encrypt(JSON.stringify(user)));
    }
    if(item == "11"){
        if(!user.stats.primary[primary]){
            user.stats.primary[primary] = 1;
        }else{
            user.stats.primary[primary]++;
        }
        if(secondary){
            if(!user.stats.secondary[secondary]){
                user.stats.secondary[secondary] = 1;
            }else{
                user.stats.secondary[secondary]++;
            }
        }

        var fntp_p = Object.keys(user.stats.primary).reduce((a, b) => obj[a] > obj[b] ? a : b);
        if(secondary)
        var fntp_s = Object.keys(user.stats.secondary).reduce((a, b) => obj[a] > obj[b] ? a : b);


        user.stats.primary_final = weapons.find(x => x.id==fntp_p)["name"];
        if(secondary)
        user.stats.secondary_final = weapons.find(x => x.id==fntp_s)["name"];

        user.stats.killstreak = 0;
        user.stats.deaths++
        user.stats.kdr = user.stats.kills / (user.stats.deaths==0 ? 1 : user.stats.kills)
        updateuser(encrypt(JSON.stringify(user)));
    }
    if(item === "io-init") {
        let cvs = document.getElementById("gameCanvas");
        width = cvs.clientWidth;
        height = cvs.clientHeight;
            $(window).resize(function() {
                width = cvs.clientWidth;
                height = cvs.clientHeight;
            });
            cvs.addEventListener("mousemove", e => {
                mouseX = e.clientX;
                mouseY = e.clientY;
            });
        }
    if(item === '1' && myPlayer.id == null) {
        myPlayer.id = data[1]
        console.log("my player id is " + data[1])
    }
    if (item == "33") {
        enemiesNear = [];
        for(let i = 0; i < data[1].length / 13; i++) {
            let playerInfo = data[1].slice(13*i, 13*i+13);
            if(playerInfo[0] == myPlayer.id) {
                prevX = myPlayer.x
                prevY = myPlayer.y
                myPlayer.x = playerInfo[1];
                myPlayer.y = playerInfo[2];
                myPlayer.dir = playerInfo[3];
                myPlayer.object = playerInfo[4];
                myPlayer.weapon = playerInfo[5];
                myPlayer.clan = playerInfo[7];
                myPlayer.isLeader = playerInfo[8];
                myPlayer.hat = playerInfo[9];
                myPlayer.accessory = playerInfo[10];
                myPlayer.isSkull = playerInfo[11];
                direc = Math.atan2(myPlayer.y-prevY, myPlayer.x-prevX);
                if(!allies.find(ally => ally.id==myPlayer.id))allies.push(myPlayer)
            } else {
                enemy.x = playerInfo[1];
                enemy.y = playerInfo[2];
                enemy.dir = playerInfo[3];
                enemy.object = playerInfo[4];
                enemy.weapon = playerInfo[5];
                enemy.clan = playerInfo[7];
                enemy.isLeader = playerInfo[8];
                enemy.hat = playerInfo[9];
                enemy.accessory = playerInfo[10];
                enemy.isSkull = playerInfo[11];
                enemiesNear.push(playerInfo);
            }
        }
    }

    if(item=="6"){
        let Object = {
            count: null,
            x: null,
            y: null,
            dir: null,
            type: null,
            owner: null,
            dir: null
        };
        var trapsNear = [];
        for(let i = 0; i < data[1].length / 8; i++){
            let ObjectData = data[1].slice(8*i, 8*i+8);
            Object.count = ObjectData[0];
            Object.x = ObjectData[1];
            Object.y = ObjectData[2];
            Object.orientation = ObjectData[4];
            Object.type = ObjectData[6];
            Object.owner = ObjectData[7];
            Object.dir = Math.atan2(Object.y-myPlayer.y, Object.x-myPlayer.x);
            if(objects.indexOf(Object)==-1){
                objects.push(Object)
            }
            if(Object.type==15 || Object.type=="15"){
                trapsNear.push(Object);
            }

            var temp2 = {};
            for(let i = 0; i < objects.length; i++){
                if(objects[i].type=="15" && !allies.find(ally => ally.id==objects[i].owner) && myPlayer.id!=objects[i].owner){
                    var weapon = weapons.find(wep => wep.id==primary);
                    obj = objects[i];
                    nearestTrap = trapsNear.sort((a,b) => distance(a.x, a.y, myPlayer.x, myPlayer.y) - distance(b.x, b.y, myPlayer.x, myPlayer.y))[0];
                    if(Math.sqrt(Math.pow((nearestTrap.x-myPlayer.x), 2) + Math.pow((nearestTrap.y-myPlayer.y), 2)) < 90){
                        nearestTrapAngle = Math.atan2(nearestTrap.y-myPlayer.y, nearestTrap.x-myPlayer.x)
                        doNewSend(["ch", ["trap = " + toDeg(nearestTrapAngle)]]);
                        for(let i = -15; i <= 15; i++){
                            setTimeout(() => {
                                place(millType, obj.dir + toRad(180) + toRad(i));
                                place(spikeType, obj.dir + toRad(180) + toRad(i));
                            }, -15-i*3)
                        }
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            temp2.hat = myPlayer.hat;
                            var breaker2 = setInterval(() => {doNewSend(["2", [nearestTrapAngle]])})
                            var breaker = setInterval(() => {
                                if(myPlayer.x==prevX && myPlayer.y==prevY){
                                    doNewSend(["13c", [0, 40, 0]])
                                    doNewSend(["c", [1, null]])
                                    setTimeout(() => {
                                        doNewSend(["13c", [0, 11, 0]])
                                    doNewSend(["13c", [0, temp2.hat, 0]])
                                    }, weapon.speed - 300)
                                }else{
                                    clearInterval(breaker)
                                    clearInterval(breaker2)
                                    doNewSend(["13c", [0, temp2.hat, 0]])
                                    doNewSend(["ch", ["Verus broke the trap!"]])
                                    doNewSend(["c", [0, null]])
                                }
                            },weapon.speed/2)
                            }, 150)
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    if(item=="h" && data[1]==myPlayer.id){
        (function(){
            if(!healToggle)return;
            repair++
            console.log(timer)
            var tempHat;
            var healAmount = (foodType==0 ? 20 : foodType==1 ? 40 : 30)
            if(data[2]<100){
                var damage = prev - data[2]
                if(damage>0){
                    if(damage==5){
                        console.log("bull tick..")
                        tester++
                        repair = 0;
                        timer = false;
                        setTimeout(() => {place(foodType);if(tester>=2){tester = 0;setTimeout(() => {doNewSend(["13c", [0, (tempHat==7||tempHat==0 ? 12 : tempHat), 0]])},10)}},200)
                    }else{
                        if(damage>50 || (damage==50&&enemy.weapon==15)){
                            console.log("equip bull")
                            tempHat = myPlayer.hat;
                            doNewSend(["13c", [0, 7, 0]])
                        }
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            for(let i = 0; i < damage/healAmount; i++){
                                place(foodType)
                            }
                        },damage>50||(damage==50&&enemy.weapon==15) ? 0 : 120)
                    }
                }
            }
            prev = data[2]
            if(timer && repair>=5){
                timer = false;
            }
        })();
    }
    if(item=="h" && data[1]==myPlayer.id){
        var hp = data[2]

        }
    isEnemyNear = false;
    if(enemiesNear) {
        nearestEnemy = enemiesNear.sort((a,b) => dist(a, myPlayer) - dist(b, myPlayer))[0];
        if(nearestEnemy){
            nearestEnemyAngle = Math.atan2(nearestEnemy.y-myPlayer.y, nearestEnemy.x-myPlayer.x);
            if(Math.sqrt(Math.pow((myPlayer.y-nearestEnemy[2]), 2) + Math.pow((myPlayer.x-nearestEnemy[1]), 2)) < 240){
                isEnemyNear = true;
            }
        }
    }
    update();
}
function toDeg(r){var p=Math.PI;return r*(180/p);}
var tester = 0;
var repair = 0;
var timer = false;
WebSocket.prototype.oldSend = WebSocket.prototype.send;
WebSocket.prototype.send = function(m){
    if (!ws){
        document.ws = this;

        ws = this;
        socketFound(this);
    }
    this.oldSend(m);
};


function socketFound(socket){
    socket.addEventListener('message', function(message){
        handleMessage(message);
    });
}
function dist(a, b){
    return Math.sqrt( Math.pow((b.y-a[2]), 2) + Math.pow((b.x-a[1]), 2) );
}
var repeater = function(key, action, interval) {
    let _isKeyDown = false;
    let _intervalId = undefined;

    return {
        start(keycode) {
            if(keycode == key && document.activeElement.id.toLowerCase() !== 'chatbox') {
                _isKeyDown = true;
                if(_intervalId === undefined) {
                    _intervalId = setInterval(() => {
                        action();
                        if(!_isKeyDown){
                            clearInterval(_intervalId);
                            _intervalId = undefined;
                            console.log("claered");
                        }
                    }, interval);
                }
            }
        },

        stop(keycode) {
            if(keycode == key && document.activeElement.id.toLowerCase() !== 'chatbox') {
                _isKeyDown = false;
            }
        }
    };


}
function toRad(angle) {
    return angle * 0.01745329251;
}
function tripleMill(){
    place(millType, direc + toRad(frozen + 100));
    place(millType, direc + toRad(frozen + 260));
    place(millType, direc + toRad(frozen + 180));
}
function distance(p1x, p1y, p2x, p2y){
    return Math.sqrt(Math.pow((p1y-p2y), 2) + Math.pow((p1x-p2x), 2))
}
const healer = repeater(81, () => {place(foodType)}, 0);
const boostPlacer = repeater(70, () => {place(boostType)}, 0);
const spikePlacer = repeater(86, () => {place(spikeType)}, 0);
const millPlacer = repeater(78, () => {tripleMill()}, 0);
const turretPlacer = repeater(72, () => {place(turretType)}, 0);
//const boostSpiker = repeater(71, boostSpike, 0);
document.addEventListener('keyup', (e)=>{
    spikePlacer.stop(e.keyCode);
    boostPlacer.stop(e.keyCode);
    //boostSpiker.stop(e.keyCode);
    millPlacer.stop(e.keyCode);
    turretPlacer.stop(e.keyCode);
    healer.stop(e.keyCode);
})

        spikePlacer.start(e.keyCode);
        healer.start(e.keyCode);
        boostPlacer.start(e.keyCode);
        //boostSpiker.start(e.keyCode);
        millPlacer.start(e.keyCode);
        turretPlacer.start(e.keyCode);
        if(e.keyCode==106){
            var crashIntervals = [];
            crashing = true;
            for(let i = 0; i < 1000; i++)crashIntervals.push(setInterval(function(){
                if(!ws || ws.readyState !== 1) return clearInterval(crashIntervals.shift());
                let crash = new Uint8Array(50);
                for(let i = 0; i <crash.length;i++){
                    crash[i] = Math.floor(Math.random()*278);
                }
                ws.send(crash);
            }))
        }
